## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

# Chromium Blink Rendering Pipeline: Style to Paint

## Your Task

Trace how a CSS style change propagates through Chromium's Blink rendering engine. Find the key C++ source files in `chromium/chromium` that implement the rendering pipeline stages: 1. The file under `third_party/blink/renderer/core/css/resolver/` that implements `StyleResolver` — the class that resolves computed styles for DOM elements. 2. The file under `third_party/blink/renderer/core/layout/` that defines `LayoutObject` — the base class for the layout tree. 3. The file that implements `PaintLayer` — the painting layer abstraction under `third_party/blink/renderer/core/paint/`. 4. The file that defines `DisplayItemList` or `PaintController` — the display list that records paint operations. Report each file path and key class name.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/chromium--2d05e315` (chromium/chromium)

Perfect! I've successfully traced the CSS style change propagation through Chromium's Blink rendering engine. Here's what I found:

## Summary of Key Files and Classes

The rendering pipeline consists of five critical components:

1. **StyleResolver** (`third_party/blink/renderer/core/css/resolver/style_resolver.h`)
   - Resolves computed styles for DOM elements
   - Maintains a 1-1 relationship with Document
   - Uses `ResolveStyle()` to compute final styles

2. **LayoutObject** (`third_party/blink/renderer/core/layout/layout_object.h`)
   - Base class for the layout tree
   - Implements layout calculation based on computed styles
   - Inherits from DisplayItemClient to connect to painting

3. **PaintLayer** (`third_party/blink/renderer/core/paint/paint_layer.h`)
   - Represents layers in the paint tree
   - Manages special rendering properties (transforms, filters, positioning)
   - Controls painting operations for each layer

4. **PaintController** (`third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/paint_controller.h`)
   - Orchestrates the painting process
   - Manages display items and caching
   - Records and sequences paint operations

5. **DisplayItemList** (`third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/display_item_list.h`)
   - Container for display items of various types
   - Stores complete paint operation list in compact format
   - Part of PaintArtifact produced by PaintController

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json` with complete file paths, class symbols, the chain of components, and a detailed narrative explanation of how CSS styles propagate through the rendering pipeline.

`third_party/blink/renderer/core/css/resolver/style_resolver.h`, the `StyleResolver` class is responsible for resolving computed styles for DOM elements. It maintains a 1-1 relationship with Document and uses methods like `ResolveStyle()` to compute the final styles based on CSS rules, cascade, and inheritance.\\n\\n2. **Layout Tree** (LayoutObject): The base class `LayoutObject` in `third_party/blink/renderer/core/layout/layout_object.h` represents the layout tree structure. Each DOM element with a corresponding LayoutObject is laid out based on its computed style. LayoutObject inherits from both GarbageCollected and DisplayItemClient, establishing the connection to the painting system.\\n\\n3. **Paint Layers** (PaintLayer): The `PaintLayer` class in `third_party/blink/renderer/core/paint/paint_layer.h` represents layers in the paint tree. PaintLayer objects are created for elements that require special rendering properties (positioning, transforms, filters, etc.). Each PaintLayer manages its layout object and controls the painting operations for that layer.\\n\\n4. **Paint Controller** (PaintController): Defined in `third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/paint_controller.h`, the `PaintController` class orchestrates the painting process. It manages display items, handles caching, and records paint operations. The PaintController maintains the current paint chunk properties and controls the serialization of display items.\\n\\n5. **Display List** (DisplayItemList): The `DisplayItemList` class in `third_party/blink/renderer/platform/graphics/paint/display_item_list.h` is a container for display items of various types. It stores the complete list of paint operations in a compact format, which can be replayed to generate the final rasterized output. The DisplayItemList is part of the PaintArtifact produced by PaintController.\\n\\nThe pipeline flows as: CSS Style \u2192 StyleResolver \u2192 ComputedStyle \u2192 LayoutObject \u2192 PaintLayer \u2192 PaintController \u2192 DisplayItemList \u2192 Rasterization. Each stage transforms the style information into the next representation, ultimately producing a list of paint operations ready for the compositor.\"\n}\n",
